commit 58ef2141496778a1ed24c0c0e253ab2762397775
Author: Tom Wiesing <tkw01536@gmail.com>
Date:   Fri Apr 30 21:26:53 2021 +0200

    ASTBuilder: Update unknown fields handling
    
    This commit updates the behavior when the simplifier encounters an
    unknown field. Previously, this field was thrown away, leading to
    incompatibilities when a new field is introduced.
    
    Instead, the code now throws a warning and keeps the field anyways. It
    also updates the list of known fields.

commit 27660d8b5e5a9d47cb6d304fe9792e8f8cb90f70
Author: Tom Wiesing <tkw01536@gmail.com>
Date:   Fri Apr 23 09:10:06 2021 +0200

    Add an AST Annotation Stage
    
    Previously, the in-progress rewrite of the query engine consisted of
    three stages: AST Generation, Query Plan Generation and Plan Execution.
    This commit inserts a new stage between the AST and Query Plan
    Generation Stages.
    
    This stage annotates the AST with all relevant information (such as
    relevant adapters and bundles) so that the query planner does not need
    to lookup adapters but can just use the already searched information.

commit 4b83c51d4cd89338ae94dd42e3a0017de368d53b
Author: Tom Wiesing <tkw01536@gmail.com>
Date:   Fri Jan 22 15:11:47 2021 +0100

    Rewrite Querying Implementation
    
    For historical reasons, the implementation made several assumptions
    about the query structure being flat. Instead of attempting to implement
    support for the nested queries added in recent versions of Drupal, this
    commit instead rewrites the query implementation based on the current
    SQL Query implementation.
    
    These changes were implemented jointly with several others during the
    WissKI Hackathon in late 2020 and subsequent WissKI HackDays.
    Thanks to everyone who participated, but in particular:
    
    Arne Fitschen <fitschen@ub.uni-heidelberg.de>
    Myriel Fichtner <myriel.fichtner@uni-bayreuth.de>
    Mark Fichtner <m.fichtner@wiss-ki.eu>

    'wisski_adapter_federated_sparql11_pb' engines, allowing users to decide
    if queries to the engine should be federated or not.

commit 234b2c2e4e2f7884f8c1fe2379e84c856e6d75e3
Author: Tom Wiesing <tkw01536@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Nov 30 15:47:15 2020 +0100

    Add \Drupal\wisski_salz\WisskiQueryBase\isFederatableSparqlQuery
    
    This commit adds a new method 'isFederatableSparqlQuery' to
    '\Drupal\wisski_salz\WisskiQueryBase' to allow queries to declare if
    they are federatable or not.
    
    This was previously done by hard-coding specific class names in
    'wisski_salz/src/Query/WisskiQueryDelegator.php' and
    'wisski_salz/src/Query/WisskiQueryBase.php'. This commit updates the
    previously hard-coded classes to make appropriate declarations.

commit d50cbc44c6e536f7c61ae48792cc82069b9bbed3
Author: Tom Wiesing <tkw01536@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Nov 30 14:35:10 2020 +0100

    Rename Sparql11TriplesTabController -> wisski_salzTriplesTabController
    
    This commit moves the Sparql11TriplesTabController from the
    'wisski_adapter_sparql11_pb' module to the generic 'wisski_salz' module.
    This is because it not longer implies any adapter-specific
    functionality.

commit f3abf3777f333f117a9f32eb0e2b7fd8bc447c45
Author: Tom Wiesing <tkw01536@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Nov 30 12:36:35 2020 +0100

    Add Drupal\wisski_salz\EngineBase\supportsTriples
    
    To avoid creating multiple "Triple" tabs on WissKI entities this commit
    reworks the existing Sparql11TriplesTabController. In particular, it
    adds a new capability declaration supportsTriples to the
    'Drupal\wisski_salz\EngineBase' class. This method allows engines to
    declare if they support displaying triples comprising to an entity and
    by default returns false.
    
    This commit also marks wisski_adapter_federated_sparql11_pb and
    wisski_adapter_sparql11_pb engines as supporting the display of triples.
    This corresponds to the legacy behavior.

commit 979c0d15f7618b0f9a9915884daf9ff0c6ecdd88
Author: Tom Wiesing <tkw01536@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Nov 30 11:19:12 2020 +0100

    Add Drupal\wisski_salz\EngineBase\supportsOntology
    
    To avoid hard-coding names of engines into WisskiOntologyForm, this
    commit adds a new method 'supportsOntology' to the
    'Drupal\wisski_salz\EngineBase' class. This method allows engines to
    declare if they support loading ontologies and by default returns false.
    
    This commit also marks wisski_adapter_federated_sparql11_pb and
    wisski_adapter_sparql11_pb engines as supporting the loading of
    ontologies. This corresponds to the legacy behavior.

commit 0c0938d828e4b9396327c4707dcd5db91ba92911

Date:   Mon Nov 30 10:57:09 2020 +0100

    Create wisski_adapter_federated_sparql11_pb module
    
    This commit creates a new 'wisski_adapter_federated_sparql11_pb' module
    that is a trimmed down copy of 'wisski_adapter_sparql11_pb'.

commit 5b39a96b20c3057b13f381200da29b058be8bf1a
Author: Tom Wiesing <tkw01536@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Nov 30 12:42:49 2020 +0100

    Sparql11TriplesTabController: Use dumpValue
    
    A regression was introduced by updating to a newer version of EasyRDF.
    In particular the getValue on certain EasyRDF objects no longer exists.
    
    This commit fixes the issue by using the dumpValue method instead.

commit dc948da83fc1fc6a597057a36dec5a84abce85dc
Author: Tom Wiesing <tkw01536@gmail.com>
Date:   Mon Nov 30 14:59:26 2020 +0100

    Sparql11Engine: Increase Basic Auth Header length
    
    When setting an HTTP Authentication Header for a triple store
    Sparql11Engine used a TextField. The default maximum length for a
    TextField is 128. This turned out to cause a problem when the username
    or password grows to long.
    
    This commit increases the maximum length for the HTTP Authentication
    Header Setting to 9999.

Date:   Thu Mar 29 12:14:13 2018 +0200

    Make the import batch-able, allow use of Drupal db
    
    By specifying how much items per batch run are processed, import
    goes into batch mode.
    
    In the xml script, you can use <connection use_drupal_db="true">
    instead of the other db connection tags. This will tell import
    to reuse Drupal's DB connection.
